 Addressing the gathering organized at this place associated with the story of 'mahabharata', Modi said, 'I appeal to you to give a decisive majority
 hamen kam se kam 300 khile hue camel dijie
 i promise that i will give you a very stable government
 ' modi ne kaha, 'aapane in logon (congress) ko 60 varsh die
 Give us at least 60 months and then see
 aap kam se kam mere liye yah kiijie
 Modi alleged that the Congress was stuck in the way of bringing back billions of rupees lying in foreign banks
 modi ne kaha, 'congress hi kaala dhan waapas laane kii raah main roda sabit ho rahi he
 If we come to power, we will enact a law and i will do everything to bring back the black money stashed in foreign banks
 ' modi ne congress upaadhyaksh rahul gandhi par nishaanaa saadhaa or rahul ke bahanoi robert wadra ke bhoomi saude par uthe vivaad par bhi nishaanaa banaaya
 Without naming anyone, Modi said that the hands of Congress leaders have turned black in the Colgate scam
 canada ke kelgeri shahar or iske aasapaas ke ilaakon se kareeb 1,00,000 logon ko baadh ke kaaran apane ghar khaali karke anyatra janaa padaa he
 The comments pashchimi canada main baari barish ke kaaran bo or albo nadiyon main jalastr badhane se baadh aa gai he
 Schools have been closed and the army has been sent for rescue operations in dozens of helicopters
 gharon ko khaali karaane ke liye 1200 sainikon ko bheja gaya he
 Kelgeri Mayor Nasheed Nenshi on Friday appealed to the people to collect their belongings and evacuate the area
 unhone logon se kuch dinon ke liye apane gharon se dur rahane ko kaha tha
 The police also went through the streets and announced with a loudspeaker about the order to evacuate the area
 shahar ke kuch ilaakon main vidyut aapurti baadhit ho gai he or kai sadaken evam pul band ho gaye hai
 Due to heavy rains in western Canada, the Bow and Elbow rivers have been flooded due to rising water levels
 skulon ko band kar diya gaya he or darjanon helicopteron main sena ko bachaav kaary ke liye bheja gaya he
 1200 soldiers have been sent to evacuate the houses
 kelgeri ke mahayor nashid nenshi ne shuukravaar ko logon se apana saamaan ekatra karne or ilaake ko khaali karne kii apil kii thi
 He asked people to stay away from their homes for a few days

 The Modi government is preparing to change the base year of GDP
 Governments vary from time to time to measure the base year of GDP
 The base year was changed to 2011-12, five years before the new base year for government gross domestic product (GDP) ( Base year)
 isko lekar tamaam tarah kii charchaaen shuru ho gai hai
 Continuing low growth in GDP has been a matter of concern for the Modi government, in such a situation, the opposition often starts making a lot of hue and cry over any of its steps
 pichley saal jab centre sarkaar ne jidipi ke valuation ke tareeke main badlaav kiya tha to isaki kaaphi aalochana hui thi
 Let's know what is GDP and what is the base year game
 sankhyikee evam kaarykram kriyanvayan mantralay (MOSPI) jidipi ke liye 2017-18 ko nayaa base year yani aadhaar varsh banane par vichaar kar rahaa he
 Currently, the base year of GDP is 2011-12
 MOSPI sachiv praveen shrivastav ne haal main kaha ki MOSPI rashtriya khaaton kii ek nai shrinkhalaa shuru karne ke liye kaam kar rahaa he
 Significantly, in the april-june quarter of this year, the growth rate of the country's gross domestic product (GDP) has come down to 5 percent
 kareeb 7 saal main bharat ke vikaas dar kii yah sabase sust raftaar he
 The important thing is that we have also lagged behind Bangladesh and Nepal in terms of GDP
 pichley paanch saal (2014-15 se 2018-19) main bharat kii ausat jidipi badhat dar 7
 It has been only 6 percent
 kya hota he gdpkisi desh kii seemaa main ek nirdhaarit samay ke bheetar taiyaar sabhi vastuon or sevaaon ke kul maudrik yaa bazaar mulya ko sakal gharelu utpaada (GDP) kehete hai
 It is a comprehensive measurement of a country's domestic production and it shows the health of a country's economy
 isaki gananaa aamtaur par salanaa hoti he, lekin bharat main ise har teen maheene yani timahi bhi aanka jaataa he
 GDP is of two types: nominal GDP and real GDP
 nominal jidipi sabhi aankadon kaa ek kaccha yoga hota he, lekin real jidipi main mahangaai ke asar ko bhi samyojit kar liya jaataa he
 That is, if the price of a commodity has increased by 10 rupees and inflation is 4 percent, then its real value will be considered as 6 percent
 bharat main jo aankade jari kiye jate hai vah real jidipi ke hote hai
 GDP is the biggest measure of a country's economic development
 agar jidipi badhata he to iskaa matlab he ki arthvyavastha zyada rojgaar paidaa kar rahi he
 It also means that the economic prosperity of the people is increasing
 kaise hoti he jidipi kii gananabharat main jidipi kii gananaa timahi-dar-timahi hoti he
 Per capita GDP comes out when GDP is divided by the national population
 bharat main krishi, udyog or seva teen ahm hisse hai, jinke aadhaar par jidipi tay kii jaati he
 For this, whatever personal consumption is done in the country, the amount invested in business and the amount of money the government spends within the country are added to all of them
 iske alaava kul niryaat main se kul aayaat ko gata diya jaataa he or is tarah jo aankada saamne aata he, use bhi upar kiye gaye kharch main jod diya jaataa he
 This is the total GDP of the country
 koun tay karata he gdpjidipi ko naapane kii jimmedaari sankhyikee or kaarykram kriyanvayan mantralay ke tahat aane vaale central statisticks offis yani kendriya sankhyikee karyaalay kii he
 It is this office that collects data from all over the country and releases their GDP figures by calculating them
 kyon badalata rahata he aadhaar varshjidipi ko tay karne ke liye aadhaar varsh tay kiye jate hai
 That is, how much the size of the economy has increased or decreased compared to the total production of the country in that base year, it is considered as the rate of GDP
 sarkaar samay-samay par base year main badlaav isliye karti he taaki desh kii arthvyavastha ke bare main aankadon kaa duniya ke hisaab se talmail rakhaa ja sake
 It is believed that the base year should be changed every five years for an accurate assessment of the economy
 saal 2015 main sarkaar ne jidipi siries kaa base year 2004-05 se badalakar 2011-12 kar diya tha
 Why is the dispute Last year, the government had made some changes in the way of calculation in GDP, there was a dispute about it
 asal main sarkaar ne kaha tha ki base year badalane ke baad uske pichley varshon main jari jidipi aankadon main bhi badlaav kiye jane chahie
 The government had issued back series on this basis for fair comparison, and because of this the GDP figures between FY 2006 and 2012 were cut, whereas those were the years of high GDP of Manmohan Singh

 The old 500 rupees of demonetised notes of 500, 1000 rupees, even after March 31, will be considered as penalty under the law, on which fine of Rs 10,000 or five times the amount kept will be imposed whichever is higher
 adhyayan evam anusandhan karne vaale shodharthi adhik se adhik 25 kii sankhya main yah note apane paas rakh sakate hai

 Under the Specified Banknotes (abolition of Liability) Ordinance-2016, it is a legal offense to keep and transact large denomination notes which are out of circulation, with a minimum penalty of Rs 10,000
 sarkaar ke ek sheersh adhikari ne bataaya ki puraane pratibandhit noton ko kaarobaar ke liye istemaal se rokane ke liye yah adhyadesh jaruri tha

 The Finance Ministry said in a statement that such nris are also required to submit the details filed in the Customs Department while depositing the closed notes in the designated branches of the Reserve Bank, at a minimum of Rs 50,000 on the false statement or in the total value of the notes presented
 The penalty will be higher
 sarkaar ne aath november ko notebandi kii ghoshnaa ke samay janata ko pratibandhit note bainkon main jamaa karwaane ke liye 50 din kaa samay diya tha
 This period was completed on Friday 30 December

 beete kai saalon se pashchim bengal main raajnneetik vajood ke liye sangharsh kar rahi bhartiya janata party (bijepi) ne is loksabhaa chunaav main aakhirkaar mamata banerjee ke garh main send laga di
 The BJP, which won only 17 percent of the votes and 2 seats in 2014, won 18 seats in West Bengal in this Lok Sabha election
 jabaki sattadhari party trinmul congress (tiemasi) kii siten ghatakar 22 rah gayi
 If you look at the vote share in Bengal, then BJP has won against Mamata and its base has also increased
 is loksabhaa chunaav main bijepi ko jahaan 40
 While 25 percent votes have been received, TMC has got 43 percent more votes
 28 fisadi vot mili
 Left party CPI less than 1 percent and CPM 6 in Bengal
 28 fisadi vot mili
 At the same time, the Congress had to be satisfied with only 5 percent votes
 purulia, bankuda, jhaadgram darjeeling, jalpaigudi or alipuradwar jaise ilaakon main party ko vyapak samarthan mila
 BJP got the reward of hard work BJP President Amit Shah had a target of 23 seats in West Bengal before the election, out of which he won 18
 pashchim bengal main bijepi kaa janaadhar majboot karne or bijepi ko tiemasi ke vikalp ke taur par pesh karne ke liye piem modi or amit shah ne jamkar pasinaa bahaya or vahaan kul 34 reliyaan kii
 Now BJP has got its result in 18 seats
 is dauraan bengal main tiemasi-bijepi kaaryakartaaon main khub hinsak sangharsh dekhne ko mila jisamen kai logon kii maut hui
 These results in favor of BJP in West Bengal have drawn lines of concern on Mamta Banerjee's forehead
 haar ko sweekaar karte hue siem mamata banerjee ne bijepi ko jeet ke liye badhai di or kaha puure parinaam aane ke baad vah is par party kaaryakartaaon ke bich chintan karengi
 Why Mamata's Fortress After the great victory of the BJP, the biggest question about West Bengal is in the minds of the people, how did the BJP finally break into the fortress of Mamta Banerjee, who is considered the lioness of Bengal
 mamata banerjee bijepi ke badhate prabhaav ko lekar ek baar aarope laga chuki thim ki aisa lagata he bengal main bijepi, congress or left ke bich koi sikret deal hui he jo mere khilaaf he
 This means that Mamata knew that the bjp's influence in West Bengal was increasing and the core voters of the Left and Congress were also shifting towards it
 jo chunaav parinaam aae hai wo bhi is baat kii tasdik kar rahe hai
 The core voters of left parties like CPM and CPI overwhelmingly voted in favor of BJP, while Congress voters now feel that BJP is the only option against Mamata in the state, so they voted openly
 enarasi or avaidh bangladeshiyon ke mudde ne mamata ko di chotpaschim bengal or kolkata main bangladesh se aane vaale avaidh nagarikon (muslim) ko lekar mamata banerjee kaa rukh hameshaa naram jabaki enarasi ko lekar garam rahaa he
